embeds HTTPClientConfig with TLSConfig\n- RemoteReadConfig - embeds HTTPClientConfig with TLSConfig\n- ScrapeConfig - embeds HTTPClientConfig with TLSConfig\n- TracingConfig - has TLSConfig field\n- AlertmanagerConfig - embeds HTTPClientConfig with TLSConfig\n\n**Service Discovery plugins with TLS:**\n- discovery/aws/ec2.go - HTTPClientConfig with TLSConfig\n- discovery/aws/lightsail.go - HTTPClientConfig with TLSConfig\n- discovery/azure/azure.go - HTTPClientConfig with TLSConfig\n\nFor outbound connections, storage/remote/write.go and storage/remote/client.go handle TLS configuration through HTTPClientConfig when establishing connections to remote endpoints, while tracing/tracing.go applies TLSConfig directly to tracing exporters. The web server uses ServeMultiple from prometheus/exporter-toolkit in web/web.go for inbound TLS handling.
